style="font-family:inherit;font-size:14pt;font-weight:bold;">CFO Commentary on Fourth-Quarter and Full Year 2013 Results</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">Summary</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The fourth quarter came in consistent with expectations.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For the fourth quarter revenue came in at $13.8B, up 3% from a year ago. PC Client Group revenue grew 2% quarter over quarter and was flat from a year ago. Our Data Center Group grew 3% quarter over quarter and 8% from a year ago. Relative to our expectations at the beginning of the quarter we saw higher PC Client Group revenue slightly offset by slower growth in our Data Center Group. Gross margin of 62% was flat to the third quarter and one point above the mid-point provided in the Outlook. Operating income for the fourth quarter was $3.5B which was up 12% from a year ago. Earnings per share was 51 cents which is up 6% from a year ago. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">For full year 2013 revenue was $52.7B, gross margin was 60%, operating income was $12.3B, net income was $9.6B, and earnings per share was $1.89. While the PC market was down on the year, we saw the market stabilize in the back half of the year with fourth quarter PC units up from a year ago. Additionally we saw strong tablet growth in the back half of the year, and inclusive of PC and tablets, our unit growth in the fourth quarter was up almost 10% from a year ago. Our Data Center Group continued to benefit from the build out of the cloud and our strong product portfolio and posted another year of growth. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The full year 2013 results when compared to the full year 2012 results were the following:</font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; Combined PC Client Group and Data Center Group platform* volumes are up 3% when compared to the third quarter. Platform* average selling prices were approximately flat when compared to the third quarter. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">PC Client Group fourth quarter revenue of $8.6B was up 2% from the third quarter with platform volumes up 3% and flat platform average selling prices. Year over year, PC Client Group revenue is flat with platform volume up 3% and platform average selling prices down 2%. On a year over year basis, desktop platform volume was up 7% and desktop platform average selling prices were up 5%. On a year on year basis, notebook platform volume is flat and notebook platform average selling prices were down 7%. </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The Data Center Group had revenue of $3.0B, up 3% from the third quarter with platform volumes down 3% and platform average selling prices up 7%. Year over year, Data Center Group revenue was up 8% with platform volume up 1% and platform average selling prices up 7%.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The other Intel architecture operating segments had revenue of $1.1B, up 4% from the third quarter. Year over year, the other Intel architecture operating segments revenue is up 9%.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:48px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:24px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The software and services operating segments had revenue of $683M, up 10% from the third quarter. Year over year, the software and services operating segments revenue was up 7%.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:24px;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Gross Margin</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Gross margin dollars were $8.6B, up approximately $200M compared to the third quarter. style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Spending for R&amp;D and MG&amp;A was $4.8B, up approximately $100M to the third quarter and up approximately $100M from the Outlook provided in October. The increase relative to the third quarter is due to an increase in R&amp;D spending and an increase in marketing on 2-in-1 devices. R&amp;D and MG&amp;A as a percentage of revenue was 35%, flat to the third quarter. Depreciation was $1.7B, in line with expectations.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Restructuring and asset impairment charges in the fourth quarter were $116M. These charges were a result of management actions to reduce workforce in response to the current business environment and to better align resources.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Amortization of acquisition related intangibles was $74M, in line with expectations.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Other Income Statement Items</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Gains and losses on equity investments and interest and other income was a net gain of $2M, lower than the $420M gain in the third quarter and flat with our Outlook of approximately zero. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The provision for taxes in the fourth quarter was at a 26.1% tax rate, up from our forecast of 25%.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Balance Sheet and Cash Flow Items</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Cash flow from operations in the fourth quarter was approximately $6.2B. During the fourth quarter we paid $1.1B in dividends, purchased $2.9B in capital assets, and repurchased $528M in stock. 2013.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div plus or minus $500M, approximately flat to 2013.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div and Intel&#8217;s ability to respond quickly to technological developments and to incorporate new features into its products. </font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; start-up costs; excess or obsolete inventory; changes in unit costs; defects or disruptions in the supply of materials or resources; product manufacturing quality/yields; and impairments of long-lived assets, including manufacturing, assembly/test and intangible assets.</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;
